# Auntie Hecker Threat Investigation Report

**Date:** July 19, 2025  
**Scope:** Analysis of files and artifacts from potential malware or threat actor activity.  
**Target:** System files dated December 7, 2019 and suspicious domain/file indicators.

---

Evidence of system-level or installer-based changes made on Dec 7, 2019 were logged. This date appears repeatedly in malware-linked activities.
